<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:center;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:center;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 12pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;">MCEWEN MINING Q2 2016 OPERATING &amp; FINANCIAL 
RESULTS</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size:
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">TORONTO, August 4, 2016 - McEwen Mining 
Inc. (NYSE: MUX) (TSX: MUX) </font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">is pleased to announce 
consolidated quarterly production of 39,555 gold equivalent ounces</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;font-size:5pt;top:-4pt;position:relative;line-
height:100%">(1)</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">, which accounts for 27,888 
ounces gold and 875,006 ounces silver. The Company reported net income of $8.4 
million</font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;font-size:5pt;top:-4pt;position:relative;line-
height:100%">(2)</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"> and $21.3 million as well as
earnings from mining operations of $19.3 million</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;font-size:5pt;top:-4pt;position:relative;line-
height:100%">(3)</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"> and $38.8 
million</font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;font-size:5pt;top:-4pt;position:relative;line-
height:100%">(3)</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"> for the three and six months
ended June 30, 2016, respectively. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">The Company generated $4.8 million and $19.5 million of 
net cash flow from operations for the three and six months ended June 30, 2016 
respectively. During the quarter we purchased a royalty on our El Gallo property
for $5.3 million which reduced our cash flow but increased our future leverage 
to higher gold and silver prices. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">We ended the second quarter of 2016 with liquid assets of
$55.7 million composed of cash of $36.7 million, precious metals of $14.3 
million and marketable securities of $4.7 million. The Company has no debt. As 
at August 2, 2016 we had liquid assets of $51.8 million.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">The tables below provide selected operating and financial
results for Q2, comparative results for Q2 2015, and our production and cost
guidance for full year 2016. </font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">For our SEC 
Form 10-Q Financial Statements and MD&amp;A please refer to: </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;">http://www.sec.gov/cgi-bin/browse-edgar?

</p>

<font style="display:inline;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>

<p style="margin:0pt 49.6pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:underline;">Operating 
&amp; Financial Highlights</font>
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt 0pt 0pt;line-height:115%;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;line-height:115%;text-indent:
-14.2pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">Production Costs&nbsp; </font>
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">Consolidated total cash costs, all-in sustaining costs 
(AISC) and all-in costs per gold equivalent ounce in Q2 were $719, $942 and
$1,201, respectively. At the El Gallo Mine total cash costs and AISC were $465 
and $495 per gold equivalent ounce, respectively. At the San Jos&#xE9; Mine 
total cash costs and AISC were $849 and $1,075 per gold equivalent ounce, 
respectively.&nbsp;&nbsp;The all-in costs per gold equivalent ounce in Q2 
include the $5.5 million purchase for the royalty on our El Gallo properties 
plus an exploration property in Mexico acquired in May 2016. These additions 
were partly offset by the $1.2 million decrease in exploration expenses as well 
as lower property holding costs incurred during 2016.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;text-indent: -14.2pt;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">Production</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">Production in Q2 totaled 39,555 gold equivalent ounces, 
which includes 15,640 gold equivalent ounces from the El Gallo Mine and 
</font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">12,352 gold ounces and 867,191 silver 
ounces</font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;"> attributable to us from our 49%</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;font-size:5pt;top:-4pt;position:relative;line-
height:100%">(4)</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"> interest in the San 
Jos&#xE9; Mine.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt 0pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-
align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>

<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;line-height:115%;text-indent:
-14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New

accounting for 23,179 gold ounces and 839,602 silver ounces.</font>

<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">Earnings from Mining Operations</font>
</p>
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">Earnings from mining operations were $19.3 million or 
$0.07 per share for Q2, compared to earnings of $13.4 million or $0.05 per share
for the six months ended June 30, 2015 (&#x201C;Q2 2015&#x201D;).</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">Cash Flow</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">Net cash provided by operations was $4.8 million or $0.02
per share for Q2, compared to net cash flow generated of $0.4 million or $nil 
per share in Q2 2015.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;line-height:115%;text-indent: 
-14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">Net Income (loss)</font>
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">Consolidated net income was $8.4 million or $0.03 per 
share for Q2, compared to a net loss of $14.1 million or $0.05 per share loss in
Q2 2015.&nbsp;&nbsp;This is a result of an increase in net income from our 
investment in Minera Santa Cruz (&#x201C;MSC&#x201D;), and lower all-in 
sustaining costs at the El Gallo Mine compared to Q2 2015. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">Average Realized Prices</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">The average realized prices of gold and silver sold 
during Q2 were $1,267 and $18.08 per ounce, respectively. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 10pt;">
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">Production and Cost Guidance</font>
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;color:#000000;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">Our 2016 production guidance remains 99,500 gold ounces 
and 3.3 million silver ounces, or approximately 144,000 gold equivalent ounces, 
at total </font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">cash costs and AISC of $780 and $935 per 
gold equivalent ounce, respectively.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;color:#000000;font-family:Times New 
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">Treasury</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 14.2pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">We ended the second quarter of 2016 with liquid assets of
$55.7 million composed of cash of $36.7 million, precious metals of $14.3 
million and marketable securities of $4.7 million.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has no
debt. As at August 2, 2016 we had liquid assets of $51.8 million.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Return of Capital (Yield)</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;color:#000000;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">The next</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;"> semi-annual 
return of capital installment of a &#xBD; cent per share will be distributed to 
shareholders of record on August 24, 2016. The distribution will be paid on 
August 29, 2016.</font>
</p>
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;color:#393939;font-family:Times New
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;color:#FF0000;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-
decoration:underline;">Redemption of Exchangeable Shares </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;color:#393939;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">At our Annual Meeting held on June 6, 2016, shareholders 
of the outstanding shares of McEwen Mining &#x2013; Minera Andes Acquisition 
Corp. (TSX:MAQ) (the &#x201C;Exchangeable Shares&#x201D;) voted to allow the 
early redemption of their shares. On August 22, 2016 we will cause each 
remaining Exchangeable Share to be redeemed in exchange for one common share of 
McEwen Mining Inc. Notice has been mailed to holders of Exchangeable Shares. 
Holders of Exchangeable Shares may continue to exercise their normal retraction 
rights at any time before August 22, 2016. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;color:#393939;font-family:Times New
Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 12pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;color:#FF0000;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;text-
decoration:underline;">El Gallo Mine, Mexico (100%)&nbsp; </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;">The El Gallo Mine </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;">delivered production results in line with guidance accounting for 
</font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">15,640 gold equivalent ounces</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">, 
compared to 17,325 gold equivalent ounces during the same period in 2015. 
Production in Q2 was lower than the prior quarter due to lower ore grades, as we
previously forecasted (2.3 gpt in Q2 2016 vs. 3.6 gpt in Q1 
2016).&nbsp;&nbsp;This decrease in the grade is the result of moving from the 
higher grade Samaniego pit to the lower grade Lupita pit. Our full year guidance
for El Gallo remains 55,000 gold equivalent ounces out of which 35,741 have been
produced in the six months ended June 30</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-size:5pt;top:-
4pt;position:relative;line-height:100%">th</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">, 
2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;As such, the rate of production will be reduced in the second 
half of the year. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">For 2016, we have budgeted $3.7 million for sustaining 
costs and capital expenditures, and $2.9 million for exploration 
activities.&nbsp;&nbsp;During Q2 we spent $1.8 million at the El Gallo Mine, 
which mostly related to an expansion of the heap leach pad that was completed 
during the second quarter of 2016, and $0.8 million in exploration activities 
aligned with our plan.&nbsp; </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>

size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 10pt;">
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:underline;">San Jos&#xE9; 
Mine, Argentina (49%)&nbsp; </font>
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">Our attributable production from San Jos&#xE9; in Q2 was 
</font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">12,352 gold ounces</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"> 
and </font><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">867,191 silver ounces</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">, 
for a total of 23,915 gold equivalent ounces. Compared to Q2 2015, gold 
production was up 10% and silver production was up 9%. </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;">Tax reforms, including the elimination of export tax on dor&#xE9; 
and concentrate, and other macroeconomic developments in Argentina, as well as 
the devaluation of the Argentinean Peso, have resulted in a significant 
improvement of operations and cash flows at </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;">San Jos&#xE9;. As a result, </font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">we received $2.8 million in 
dividends from MSC</font><font style="display:inline;font-
family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-size:5pt;top:-
4pt;position:relative;line-height:100%">(4) </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">in
Q2 and we have received $5.4 million in dividends year-to-date against an 
original dividend forecast of $7.5 million for 2016 (in comparison, the Company 
received $500,000 in dividends for all of 2015).&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company expects 
to receive additional dividends throughout the year provided gold and silver 
prices remain at current or higher levels. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">The 2016 exploration budget has been increased from $4.5 
million to $6.5 million. This is the first time in several years that a 
significant budget has been allocated to exploration</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:10pt;">.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;text-decoration:underline;">Gold Bar 
Advanced-Stage Project</font><font style="display:inline;font-

</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-

</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-

<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-

below (see chart below). </font>

<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">The Company estimates that we will receive a permitting 
decision from the Bureau of Land Management during the first quarter of 
2017.&nbsp;&nbsp;This final permit, once received, will allow us to begin 
construction of the mine, which we have estimated to take 12 months. Production 
is estimated to begin the following year in 2018. For 2016, we have budgeted 
approximately $4.7 million to be spent towards advancing the project closer to 
the production stage, of which $1.3 million has been spent during the six month 
period ended June 30, 2016.&nbsp;&nbsp;Mine permitting and engineering 
activities continue to advance at Gold Bar.&nbsp; </font>

<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-

</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.15pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-

<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>

<p style="margin:0pt 14.15pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-

10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:10pt;">The Company is preparing an updated Preliminary Economic 
Assessment (&#x201C;PEA&#x201D;) for Los Azules.&nbsp; We believe the recent 
policy shifts in Argentina such as the elimination of export taxes, the 
devaluation of the peso and the lifting of certain import restrictions on 
equipment will improve the economics of Los Azules over the previously published
PEA completed in 2013.&nbsp; For 2016, we have budgeted $1.0 million to advance 
the project, and will commence a drill program in early 2017.&nbsp;

<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">About McEwen Mining</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
weight:bold;color:#262626;font-size:10pt;"> &nbsp;(</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-

</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-
family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt 14.2pt 0pt 0pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">McEwen Mining&#x2019;s goal is to 
qualify for inclusion in the S&amp;P 500 Index by creating a high growth, 
profitable gold and silver producer focused in the Americas and Europe. McEwen 
Mining's principal assets consist of the San Jos&#xE9; Mine in Santa Cruz, 
Argentina (49% interest), the El Gallo Mine and El Gallo Silver project in 
Sinaloa, Mexico, the Gold Bar project in Nevada, USA, and the Los Azules copper 
project in San Juan, Argentina.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
size: 10pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:10pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 10pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:10pt;">McEwen Mining has a total of 299 million
shares outstanding and 305 million fully diluted. Rob McEwen, Chairman and Chief
Owner, owns 25% of the Company.</font>
</p>

ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:9pt;">Minera Santa Cruz S.A., the owner of the San Jos&#xE9; 
Mine, is responsible for and has supplied to the Company all reported results 
from the San Jos&#xE9; Mine. McEwen Mining&#x2019;s joint venture partner, a 
subsidiary of Hochschild Mining plc, and its affiliates other than MSC do not 
accept responsibility for the use of project data or the adequacy or accuracy of
this release. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:9pt;">CAUTIONARY NOTE REGARDING NON-GAAP 
MEASURES </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:9pt;">In this report, we have provided information prepared or 
calculated according to U.S. GAAP, as well as some non-U.S. GAAP ("non-GAAP") 
performance measures. Because the non-GAAP performance measures do not have any 
standardized meaning prescribed by U.S. GAAP, they may not be comparable to 
similar measures presented by other companies. </font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:9pt;">Total Cash Costs and All-in Sustaining 
Costs</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:9pt;">Total cash costs consist of mining, processing, on-site 
general and administrative costs, community and permitting costs related to 
current explorations, royalty costs, refining and treatment charges (for both 
dor&#xE9; and concentrate products), sales costs, export taxes and operational 
stripping costs. All-in sustaining cash costs consist of total cash costs (as 
described above), plus environmental rehabilitation costs, amortization of the 
asset retirement costs related to operating sites, sustaining exploration and 
development costs, and sustaining capital expenditures. In order to arrive at 
our consolidated all-in sustaining costs, we also include corporate general and 
administrative expenses. Depreciation is excluded from both total cash costs and
all-in sustaining cash costs. For both total cash costs and all-in </font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:9pt;"></font></p></div><div style="margin-left:5.71895424836601%;margin-
right:6.04575163398693%;">
<p><font size="1"> </font></p><div style="width:100%">
style="border-collapse:collapse;width: 100.00%;margin-left:0pt;">

size: 12pt;">
<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-
&nbsp;
</p>
</div></div><div style="margin-left:5.71895424836601%;margin-
right:6.04575163398693%;"><p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-
justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 
9pt;"><font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:9pt;">sustaining costs we include our attributable share of total cash 
costs from operations where we hold less than a 100% economic share in the 
production, such as MSC, where we hold a 49% interest.&nbsp;&nbsp;Total cash 
cost and all-in sustaining cash cost per ounce sold are calculated on a co-
product basis by dividing the respective proportionate share of the total cash 
costs and all-in sustaining cash costs for the period attributable to each metal
by the ounces of each respective metal sold. We use and report these measures to
provide additional information regarding operational efficiencies both on a 
consolidated and an individual mine basis, and believe that these measures 
provide investors and analysts with useful information about our underlying 
costs of operations. A reconciliation to the nearest U.S. GAAP measure is 
provided in McEwen Mining's Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for the quarter ended 
June 30, 2016.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:9pt;">Earnings from Mining Operations</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
serif;font-size:9pt;">The term earnings from mining operations used in this
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
report is a non-GAAP financial measure. We use and report this measure because 
we believe it provides investors and analysts with a useful measure of the 
underlying earnings from our mining operations. We define earnings from mining 
operations as gold and silver revenues from our El Gallo 1 Mine and our 49% 
attributable share of the San Jos&#xE9; mine's net sales, less their respective 
production costs applicable to sales. To the extent that production costs 
applicable to sales may include depreciation and amortization expense related to
the fair value increments on historical business acquisitions (fair value paid 
in excess of the carrying value of the underlying assets and liabilities assumed
on the date of acquisition), we deduct this expense in order to arrive at 
production costs applicable to sales that only include depreciation and 
amortization expense incurred at the mine-site level. The San Jos&#xE9; Mine net
sales and production costs applicable to sales are presented, on a 100% basis, 
in Note 5 of McEwen Mining's quarterly report on Form 10-Q for the quarter ended
June 30, 2016.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:9pt;">Average Realized Prices</font>
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:9pt;">The term average realized price per ounce used in this 
report is also a non-GAAP financial measure. We report this measure to better 
understand the price realized in each reporting period for gold and 
silver.&nbsp;&nbsp;Average realized price is calculated as sales of gold and 
silver (excluding commercial deductions) over the number of ounces sold in the 
period.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:9pt;">Liquid Assets</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:9pt;">Liquid assets corresponds to &#x201C;cash, investments and
precious metals&#x201D;, which is also a non</font><font 
style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif;font-
size:9pt;">&#8209;GAAP financial measure. We report this measure to better 
understand our liquidity in each reporting period.&nbsp;&nbsp;Cash, investments 
and precious metals are calculated as the sum of cash, investments and ounces of
dor&#xE9; held in inventories with precious metals, valued at the London PM Fix 
spot price at the corresponding period. A reconciliation between precious metals
valued at cost and precious metals valued at market value is provided in McEwen 
Mining's Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for the quarter ended June 30th, 
2016.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:9pt;">Advanced Stage Projects</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-size:9pt;">Advanced-stage properties consist of properties for which 
a feasibility study has been completed indicating the presence of mineralized 
material, and that have obtained or are in the process of obtaining the required
permitting for construction and operation. Our designation of certain properties
as &#x201C;Advanced-stage Properties&#x201D; should not suggest that we have 
proven or probable reserves at those properties as defined by the SEC Industry 
Guide 7.&nbsp;&nbsp;In addition, as described under the &#x201C;Critical 
Accounting Policies&#x201D; section contained in our annual report on Form 10-K 
for the year ended December 31, 2015, we define &#x201C;Mine Development 
Costs&#x201D; as the costs incurred to design and construct mining and 
processing facilities, including engineering and metallurgical studies, 
drilling, and other related costs to delineate an ore body, and the removal of 
overburden to initially expose an ore body at open pit surface or underground 
mines. Since no proven and probable reserves have been established on any of our
properties except for our 49% interest in the San Jos&#xE9; mine, mine 
development costs are not capitalized at any of the our properties, but rather 
are expensed as incurred, and allocated within &#x201C;Mine Development 
Costs&#x201D; in the Consolidated Statement of Operations and Comprehensive 
Income.</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-family:Arial,Helvetica,sans-
serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:9pt;">CAUTION CONCERNING FORWARD-LOOKING 
STATEMENTS</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">
<font style="display:inline;font-size:9pt;">&nbsp;</font>
</p>
<p style="margin:0pt;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-
ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman,Times,serif;font-size: 9pt;">

expectations or beliefs as to future events and results. Forward-looking

subject to significant business, economic and competitive uncertainties, risks 
and contingencies, and there can be no assurance that such statements and

information. Risks and uncertainties that could cause results or future events 
to differ materially from current expectations expressed or implied by the 
forward-looking statements and information include, but are not limited to, 
factors associated with fluctuations in the market price of precious metals,
mining industry risks, political, economic, social and security risks associated
with foreign operations, the ability of the corporation to receive or receive in
a timely manner permits or other approvals required in connection with 
operations, risks associated with the construction of mining operations and 
commencement of production and the projected costs thereof, risks related to
